FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]

SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[NumDocument], [p].[Projet_Id], [p].[QuantiteEncre], [p].[QuantiteVernis], [p].[ReferenceArticleSup], [p0].[Id], [p0].[DateDebut], [p0].[DateFin], [p0].[DateLivraisonPrev], [p0].[Description], [p0].[Intitule], [p0].[NumeroDossier], [p0].[ReferenceArticle], [p0].[ReferenceClient], [p0].[TypeDescription], [p0].[id_typeprojet], [p0].[chargeCompte], [p0].[quantite], [t].[Id], [t].[Abrege], [t].[Intitule], [t].[Reference], [s0].[Id], [s0].[DateCreation], [s0].[Laize], [s0].[machine], [s0].[MetrageLineaire], [s0].[NumPiece], [s0].[Passe], [s0].[Pf_id], [s0].[QuantiteSupport], [s0].[quantite], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Bon_id], [s0].[DateAffection], [s0].[Pourcentage], [s0].[QuantiteUtilise], [s0].[ReferenceMP], [s0].[TypeId], [s0].[Id00], [s0].[Label]
FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]

LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]

) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]

FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]

SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[NumDocument], [p].[Projet_Id], [p].[QuantiteEncre], [p].[QuantiteVernis], [p].[ReferenceArticleSup], [p0].[Id], [p0].[DateDebut], [p0].[DateFin], [p0].[DateLivraisonPrev], [p0].[Description], [p0].[Intitule], [p0].[NumeroDossier], [p0].[ReferenceArticle], [p0].[ReferenceClient], [p0].[TypeDescription], [p0].[id_typeprojet], [p0].[chargeCompte], [p0].[quantite], [t].[Id], [t].[Abrege], [t].[Intitule], [t].[Reference], [s0].[Id], [s0].[DateCreation], [s0].[Laize], [s0].[machine], [s0].[MetrageLineaire], [s0].[NumPiece], [s0].[Passe], [s0].[Pf_id], [s0].[QuantiteSupport], [s0].[quantite], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Bon_id], [s0].[DateAffection], [s0].[Pourcentage], [s0].[QuantiteUtilise], [s0].[ReferenceMP], [s0].[TypeId], [s0].[Id00], [s0].[Label]
FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]

SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[NumDocument], [p].[Projet_Id], [p].[QuantiteEncre], [p].[QuantiteVernis], [p].[ReferenceArticleSup], [p0].[Id], [p0].[DateDebut], [p0].[DateFin], [p0].[DateLivraisonPrev], [p0].[Description], [p0].[Intitule], [p0].[NumeroDossier], [p0].[ReferenceArticle], [p0].[ReferenceClient], [p0].[TypeDescription], [p0].[id_typeprojet], [p0].[chargeCompte], [p0].[quantite], [t].[Id], [t].[Abrege], [t].[Intitule], [t].[Reference], [s0].[Id], [s0].[DateCreation], [s0].[Laize], [s0].[machine], [s0].[MetrageLineaire], [s0].[NumPiece], [s0].[Passe], [s0].[Pf_id], [s0].[QuantiteSupport], [s0].[quantite], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Bon_id], [s0].[DateAffection], [s0].[Pourcentage], [s0].[QuantiteUtilise], [s0].[ReferenceMP], [s0].[TypeId], [s0].[Id00], [s0].[Label]
FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]

FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]

LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NumPiece], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0]
